6:T435,An interview with the popular novelist Lisa: 
"Lisa, would you share your thoughts when you wrote this book?" 
"Actually, there was a time before I started work on this book when I couldn't write a single word. I was deeply troubled by a crisis of inspiration at that time. One night, I had a dream in which I was stuck on five books about different subjects which contained lots of interesting puzzles and tricks. It was an amazing journey of discovery and I got a lot of ideas out of it." 

The popular novelist suffered from a crisis of inspiration at the very time of her popularity. What kind of dream journey allowed her to let go of her anxiety and regain her inspiration? What would you do to escape a crisis of inspiration?
